28  /**
29   * Exhaustive serialization tests for all the HTML5 DTOs.
30   */
31  @SuppressWarnings({})
32  class Html5_ComboRoundTripTest extends ComboRoundTripTest_Base {
33  
34  	private static final B btag = b("bbb");
35  
36  	private static A a2(Object ref, Object...children) {
37  		return HtmlBuilder.a(ref, children);
38  	}
39  
40  	private static <T> ComboRoundTrip_Tester.Builder<T> tester(int index, String label, Type type, T bean) {
41  		return ComboRoundTrip_Tester.create(index, label, type, ()->bean);
42  	}
43  
44  	private static ComboRoundTrip_Tester<?>[] TESTERS = {
45  		tester(1, "A", A.class, a2("http://foo", "bar"))
46  			.json("{_type:'a',a:{href:'http://foo'},c:['bar']}")
47  			.jsonT("{t:'a',a:{href:'http://foo'},c:['bar']}")
48  			.jsonR("{\n\t_type: 'a',\n\ta: {\n\t\thref: 'http://foo'\n\t},\n\tc: [\n\t\t'bar'\n\t]\n}")
49  			.xml("<a href='http://foo'>bar</a>")
50  			.xmlT("<a href='http://foo'>bar</a>")
51  			.xmlR("<a href='http://foo'>bar</a>\n")
52  			.xmlNs("<a href='http://foo'>bar</a>")
53  			.html("<a href='http://foo'>bar</a>")
54  			.htmlT("<a href='http://foo'>bar</a>")
55  			.htmlR("<a href='http://foo'>bar</a>\n")
56  			.uon("(_type=a,a=(href=http://foo),c=@(bar))")
57  			.uonT("(t=a,a=(href=http://foo),c=@(bar))")
58  			.uonR("(\n\t_type=a,\n\ta=(\n\t\thref=http://foo\n\t),\n\tc=@(\n\t\tbar\n\t)\n)")
59  			.urlEnc("_type=a&a=(href=http://foo)&c=@(bar)")
60  			.urlEncT("t=a&a=(href=http://foo)&c=@(bar)")
61  			.urlEncR("_type=a\n&a=(\n\thref=http://foo\n)\n&c=@(\n\tbar\n)")
62  			.msgPack("83A55F74797065A161A16181A468726566AA687474703A2F2F666F6FA16391A3626172")
63  			.msgPackT("83A174A161A16181A468726566AA687474703A2F2F666F6FA16391A3626172")
